<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продраться.html>продра́ться</a> (22603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продраться.html>продра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продираться.html>продира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear [be worn] into holes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продраться.html>продрались</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́кти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó prodralisʹ lókti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his coat is out at the elbows</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squeeze/make/force one's way <i>(through)</i></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продрать.html>продра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продрогнуть.html>продро́гнуть</a> (18156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">drógnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продрогнуть.html>продро́гнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodrógnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрогнуть.html>дро́гнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be cold, to become frozen, to feel chilly; to freeze, to numb (by coldness), to shiver</li></ol>

***продувать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́ть</a> (19972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продуть.html>проду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">produvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продуть.html>проду́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean by blowing, to blow clean</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to catch a cold from the wind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозняк.html>сквозняко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>produvájet</b> skvoznjakóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is catching a cold from the draft</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in sports or gambling</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow through
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветерок.html>ветеро́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">veterók <b>produvál</b> kómnatu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the breeze was blowing through the room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветерок.html>ветерко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kómnatu <b>produválo</b> veterkóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the breeze was blowing through the room</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продувающий.html>продува́ющий</a> (19972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***продуктивный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продуктивный.html>продукти́вный</a> (21117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">productivus</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">productif</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">produktiv</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продуктивный.html>продукти́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">produktívnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)продукти́внее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)продукти́вней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>productive; effective, efficient; fruitful</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продуктивный.html>продукти́вно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">produktívno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">продукти́вность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">produktívnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">непродукти́вный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neproduktívnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продукт.html>проду́кт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prodúkt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">

***продуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продуть.html>проду́ть</a> (20885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продуть.html>проду́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продувать.html>продува́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clean by blowing, to blow clean</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to catch a cold from the wind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продуть.html>проду́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозняк.html>сквозняко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>prodúlo</b> skvoznjakóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he caught a cold from the draft</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for a specified amount of time</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in sports or gambling</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to run <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">a specified distance</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">продува́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">produvánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>продю́сер</a> (12565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">producer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>продю́сер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodjúsɛr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>продю́сера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>продю́серы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продюсер.html>продю́серов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(film) producer (male or female)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зд</a> (6407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезжать.html>проезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projézd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́здов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>journey
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плат.html>пла́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pláta za projézd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fare</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оплатить.html>оплати́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oplatítʹ projézd</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pay the fare</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>passage, thoroughfare
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зда</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">projézda net!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">no thoroughfare!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lane, passage</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pójezd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проездной.html>проездно́й</a> (15056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезд.html>прое́зд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projézd</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проездной.html>проездно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projezdnój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> travel; serving for travel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проездной.html>проездно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:билет.html>биле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projezdnój</b> bilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>travel</b> ticket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проездной.html>проездно́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projezdnój</b> dokumént</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>travel</b> document <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">document giving the right to travel</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***проезжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проезжать.html>проезжа́ть</a> (6376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезжать.html>проезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go through/by (by horse or vehicle), to ride through/by, to drive through/by</li>
<li>to drive past/along/across</li>
<li>to travel a certain distance</li></ol>

***проезжий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проезжий.html>прое́зжий</a> (9129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезжий.html>прое́зжий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projézžij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>passing by, through (traveller)</li>
<li>fit, used for traffic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проезжать.html>прое́зжая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projézžaja</b> častʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">carriageway</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́кт</a> (1566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Projekt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́кт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proékt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́кта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́кты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проект.html>прое́ктов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>проём</a> (5674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>прое́м</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projém</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">first-person singular future indicative of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проесть.html>прое́сть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projéstʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>проем</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projóm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span>

***проехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a> (3432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проезжать.html>проезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go through/by <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by horse or vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to ride through/by, to drive through/by</li>
<li>to drive past/along/across</li>
<li>to travel (a certain distance)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проехать.html>прое́хать</a></b> and <a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ždatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to wait for <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an amount of time; + accusative or (dated) genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жевать.html>жева́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ževátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
